    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    release_date DATE,
    platform VARCHAR(100)
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);

    headquarters VARCHAR(255)
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,

    review_text TEXT,

    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)

CREATE TABLE developer (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    founded_date DATE,
    headquarters VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE review (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,
    player_id INT,
    rating DECIMAL(2, 1),
    review_text TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES game(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)
);

CREATE TABLE player (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);</t><s>SHOW TABLES;</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));</t><s>SHOW TABLES;</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>show tables;</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>show columns from players;</s>

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>SHOW INDEX FROM achievements;</s>
